## Surprising Connections (you probably didn't know these)
- `TDD tests for actionable-items refactor.  Rules under test:   - Auto-recoverable` --uses--> `JuggleDB`  [INFERRED]
  tests/test_watchdog_actionable_items.py → src/juggle_db.py
- `First stall (watchdog_retried=0), send_task succeeds → notification only.` --uses--> `JuggleDB`  [INFERRED]
  tests/test_watchdog_actionable_items.py → src/juggle_db.py
- `retry_blocked → action item with [RQ] prefix, Decide:, and Cause:.` --uses--> `JuggleDB`  [INFERRED]
  tests/test_watchdog_actionable_items.py → src/juggle_db.py
- `retry_blocked → action item ONLY, not a passive notification as well.` --uses--> `JuggleDB`  [INFERRED]
  tests/test_watchdog_actionable_items.py → src/juggle_db.py
- `Orphan auto-recovery attempt (< max) → notification only.` --uses--> `JuggleDB`  [INFERRED]
  tests/test_watchdog_actionable_items.py → src/juggle_db.py

## Suggested Questions
_Questions this graph is uniquely positioned to answer:_

- **Why does `JuggleDB` connect `Community 0` to `Community 1`, `Community 2`, `Community 3`, `Community 4`, `Community 7`, `Community 9`, `Community 10`, `Community 12`, `Community 13`, `Community 14`, `Community 15`, `Community 16`, `Community 18`, `Community 19`, `Community 23`, `Community 24`, `Community 25`, `Community 27`, `Community 28`, `Community 29`, `Community 32`, `Community 38`, `Community 39`, `Community 41`, `Community 42`?**
  _High betweenness centrality (0.455) - this node is a cross-community bridge._
- **Why does `get_db()` connect `Community 4` to `Community 0`, `Community 7`, `Community 10`, `Community 12`, `Community 14`, `Community 16`?**
  _High betweenness centrality (0.057) - this node is a cross-community bridge._
- **Why does `JuggleTmuxManager` connect `Community 1` to `Community 2`, `Community 4`, `Community 5`, `Community 7`, `Community 8`, `Community 14`, `Community 15`, `Community 16`, `Community 18`, `Community 19`?**
  _High betweenness centrality (0.050) - this node is a cross-community bridge._
- **Are the 1274 inferred relationships involving `JuggleDB` (e.g. with `TDD tests for actionable-items refactor.  Rules under test:   - Auto-recoverable` and `First stall (watchdog_retried=0), send_task succeeds → notification only.`) actually correct?**
